***зажигаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зажигаться.html>зажига́ться</a> (13869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажигать.html>зажига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zažigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажигаться.html>зажига́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zažigátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажечься.html>заже́чься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch fire</li>
<li>to light up, <i>(electical lights)</i> to turn on, to go on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уличный.html>у́личные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фонарь.html>фонари́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зажигаться.html>зажига́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">úličnyje fonarí <b>zažigájutsja</b> v pjatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the street lights go on at five</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(eyes, face etc)</i> to light up <i>(with)</i>, to kindle <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><i>(feeling, desire etc)</i> to be seized <i>(with)</i>, to be overcome <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to get enthusiastic <i>(about, over)</i>, to get carried away <i>(by)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажигать.html>зажига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zažigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***зажимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зажимать.html>зажима́ть</a> (10991)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажимать.html>зажима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zažimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажать.html>зажа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press, to squeeze, to clutch</li>
<li>to stop up, to block up, to plug up</li>
<li>to suppress, to stifle, to restrict</li></ol>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:сжимать.html>сжима́я</a> что-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:придавливать.html>прида́вливая</a> чем-либо, <a href = vnd.unilang:плотный.html>пло́тно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрывать.html>закрыва́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>отверстие</a>) <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

***зажить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зажить.html>зажи́ть</a> (8976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажить.html>зажи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zažítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заживать.html>зажива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to heal, to close up, to skin over (of wounds)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зажить.html>зажила́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rána býstro <b>zažilá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wound has healed quickly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to begin to live (<i>only perfective</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тех</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>по́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зажить.html>за́жили</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:зажить.html>зажи́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>сча́стливо</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>счастли́во</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S tex por oní <b>zážili/zažíli</b> sčástlivo/sčastlívo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Since then they started to live happily.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зажмуриваться.html>зажму́риваться</a> (29910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зажму́ривать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zažmúrivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***зажмурить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зажмурить.html>зажму́рить</a> (14414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">жму́рить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žmúritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажмурить.html>зажму́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zažmúritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">жму́рить</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зажму́ривать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to screw up or shut one's eyes, to screw up one's eyelids</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill somebody</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажмуриться.html>зажму́риться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zažmúritʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жмуриться.html>жму́риться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажмуриваться.html>зажму́риваться</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зазеваться.html>зазева́ться</a> (17356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зевать.html>зева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зазеваться.html>зазева́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zazevátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зазёвываться</b>)

***зазывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зазывать.html>зазыва́ть</a> (21105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зазывать.html>зазыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zazyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зазвать.html>зазва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to invite <i>(persistently)</i>, to call in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shout (to someone) to come in</li></ol>

***заиграть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заиграть.html>заигра́ть</a> (8475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заиграть.html>заигра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaigrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заигрывать.html>заи́грывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to play</li>
<li>to begin to sparkle</li>
<li>to look to advantage, to stand out</li>
<li><i>(a record, tape recorder etc.)</i> to spoil/wear out by playing</li>
<li>to run down, to exhaust, to overuse, to overwear <i>(by repetition)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appropriate, to help oneself <i>(to)</i>, to hook</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заи́грывание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaígryvanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***заигрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заигрывать.html>заи́грывать</a> (21748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заиграть.html>заигра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaigrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заигрывать.html>заи́грывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaígryvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заиграть.html>заигра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flirt <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to make advances <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><i>(a record, tape recorder etc.)</i> to spoil/wear out by playing</li>
<li>to run down, to exhaust, to overuse, to overwear <i>(by repetition)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appropriate, to help oneself <i>(to)</i>, to hook</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заикаться.html>заика́вшийся</a> (9450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
